if (!is_file('includes/color_utils.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/color_utils.inc.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('includes/color_utils.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/color_utils.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/color_utils.inc.php') != 'dcb6577854e2815aa9fb4fccbb763f905e3b552f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/color_utils.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/color_utils.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/color_utils.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/color_utils.inc.php') !== 'dcb6577854e2815aa9fb4fccbb763f905e3b552f') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/color_utils.inc.php') !== '33d28a319ae4b38ba317da042872ac50f7536216') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/color_utils.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/color_utils.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/color_utils.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/color_utils.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/color_utils.inc.php') !== 'dcb6577854e2815aa9fb4fccbb763f905e3b552f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/color_utils.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') != '6b8e0889a00f5760efb44ffb8488a02fa6d0ea95') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oid_utils.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== '6b8e0889a00f5760efb44ffb8488a02fa6d0ea95') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== 'eb1e2488365eec214995dee28bf303900aa7ac8b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oid_utils.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oid_utils.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== '6b8e0889a00f5760efb44ffb8488a02fa6d0ea95') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

			if (!@copy('phpstan.neon.dist', $backup_name)) {

			}
		}

			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): phpstan.neon.dist');
